***reu.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reu.html>reu</a> (73253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">reude</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hruþjan-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hruttōn-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> root shared by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κόρυζα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóruza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hrot</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scottish_Gaelic" class="extiw" title="w:Scottish Gaelic">Scottish Gaelic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gd">cnatan</i>.  Or, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hreutan-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrūtan-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hruttōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to snore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which would be related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hrjóta</i>.
</p><p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Rüde</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reu.html>reu</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reuen.html>reuen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reus.html>reus</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reu.html>reutje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teef.html>teef</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>male dog or other canine

<p>First attested <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1601" class="extiw" title="w:1601">1601</a>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rheumatismós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ῥεῦμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rheûma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stream, flow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reus.html>reus</a> (5868)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ruese</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rese</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*riso</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*risi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*risiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">giant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Riese</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">giant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">risi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">giant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***revelatie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:revelatie.html>revelatie</a> (73248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">revelatio</i> (from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">revelatus</i>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">revelare</i> 'to reveal', itself from re- "opposite of" + velare "to cover, <a href = vnd.unilang:veilen.html>veil</a>" from velum "a <a href = vnd.unilang:veilen.html>veil</a>"), possibly <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> Middle French <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">revelaciun</i> or modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">révélation</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:revelatie.html>revelatie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:revelatie.html>revelaties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:revelatie.html>revelatietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A revelation, the act or an instance of revealing or disclosure; especially divine revelation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The divinely revelead truth, as from the Bible and/or Coran in Judeo-Christianity namely Islam</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A discovery, find, notably one who <a href = vnd.unilang:surprises.html>surprises</a> positively, e.g. with a great performance</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>(revealing) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:openbaring.html>openbaring</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onthulling.html>onthulling</a></span></li>
<li>(discovery) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontdekking.html>ontdekking</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vondst.html>vondst</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verrassing.html>verrassing</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gereveleerd</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">reveleren</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:revelatie.html>revelatie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:ontdekking.html>ontdekking</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:openbaring.html>openbaring</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:onthulling.html>onthulling</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>Onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schitterend.html>schitterende</a> goal <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jonge.html>jonge</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voetballer.html>voetballer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:revelatie.html>revelatie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:seizoen.html>seizoen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geworden.html>geworden</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***rewind.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rewind.html>rewind</a> (67791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">re-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wind</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rewind.html>rewind</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">rewinds</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">rewinding</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">rewound</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To wind (something) again.
<ul><li><b>2000</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_RR_Martin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George RR Martin">George RR Martin</a>, <i>A <a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>Storm</a> of Swords</i>, Bantam 2011, p. 535:
<dl><dd>A Myrish crossbowman poked his head out a different window, got off a bolt, and ducked down to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rewind.html>rewind</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To wind (something) back, now especially of cassette or video tape, CD, DVD etc.; to go back on a video or audio recording.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To go back or think back to a previous <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> or place, or a previous point in a discourse.
<ul><li><b>December 12 2016</b>, Editorial Team of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicago_Tribune" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Chicago Tribune">Chicago Tribune</a>, <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.chicagotribune.com/news/opinion/editorials/ct-russia-trump-putin-obama-bush-moscow-kremlin-edit-1213-jm-20161212-story.html">Editorial: Trump, Putin and the <a href = vnd.unilang:risks.html>risks</a> of a reset</a></i>
<dl><dd>To understand Russia, you have to dive deep into its history — boyars and czars, Pushkin and <a href = vnd.unilang:pasternak.html>Pasternak</a>, Stalin and Stalingrad. To understand the perils of underestimating Russia, you don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have to go back that far. Just <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rewind.html>rewind</a></b> to 2001, when George W. Bush naively sized up Vladimir Putin as a leader he could work with, a conclusion Bush reached when he looked into the Russian leader's <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> and "found him to be very straightforward and trustworthy.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rewind.html>rewind</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">rewinds</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The act of rewinding.</li>
<li>A button or other mechanism for rewinding.
<dl><dd><i>I meant to pause the picture, but hit the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rewind.html>rewind</a></b> by mistake.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***rib.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> rib (7757)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">rib</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rib</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kast.html>kast</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">case, close</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cf. similar constructions in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rib cage</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Rippenkorb</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ribbenkast.html>ribbenkast</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ribbenkasten.html>ribbenkasten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ribbenkast.html>ribbenkastje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***riche.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:riche.html>riche</a> (80014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:riche.html>riche</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ryche</i> (also <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">rike</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">rīċe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">power, authority, might, dominion, rule, empire, reign</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*rīkī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rīkiją</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">realm, power</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(<a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>)reǵ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to straighten, direct</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. 
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:rik.html>rik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rijk.html>rijk</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Reich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">rike</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">ríki</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">regnum</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">rich</span>.

***richter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:richter.html>richter</a> (26500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:richten.html>richten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:richter.html>richter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:richter.html>richters</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:richteren.html>richteren</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">aimer</span>, one who aims (e.g. a projectile weapon)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Protestantism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> biblical judge <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the usual plural <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:richteren.html>richteren</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">sjofeet</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> official of the court of justice overseeing the implementation of verdicts, without having a voice in them <span class="defdate">[before 1800]</span></li></ol>
